### [355] [Neuro-evolutionary stochastic architectures in gauge-covariant neural fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20373)
*Rodrigo Carmo Terin*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 本文在规范协变随机神经场框架中引入函数空间演化的慢随机变量，构建有效理论。通过最大李雅普诺夫指数、放大因子和谱核等对称性约束诊断，并结合U(1)马尔可夫进化方案。实验发现，完全对称约束的Ginibre U(1)版本能稳健逼近近边际区域并复现低频有限宽度谱行为，支持将对称性引导的有效稳定性诊断作为随机架构搜索的实用原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将架构级参数提升为函数空间中演化的慢随机变量，以扩展规范协变随机神经场框架，从而更好地理解有限宽度效应和边际性，并为随机架构搜索提供理论指导。

Method: 提出有效理论（经典交换场），通过最大李雅普诺夫指数、放大因子和谱核提供对称性约束的边际性与有限宽度效应诊断；引入与局部U(1)结构兼容的马尔可夫进化方案；将基因型简化为权重方差σ_w²，适应度函数结合谱一致性、边际稳定性和对称性约束临界锚点；比较三种进化模型。

Result: 完全对称约束的Ginibre U(1)版本稳健地逼近窄近边际区域，并成功复现预测的低频有限宽度谱行为；其他两种模型未能实现此效果。

Conclusion: 对称性引导的有效稳定性诊断可作为随机架构搜索的实用原则，在受控环境中具有应用价值。

Abstract: We extend our gauge-covariant stochastic neural-field framework by promoting architecture-level parameters to slow stochastic variables evolving in function space. Our effective theory is formulated in terms of classical commuting fields and provides symmetry-constrained diagnostics of marginality and finite-width effects through the maximal Lyapunov exponent, the amplification factor, and dressed spectral kernels. On top of this dynamics, we introduce a Markovian evolutionary scheme compatible with the local $U(1)$ structure of the effective model. By using a minimal implementation, the genotype is reduced to the weight-variance parameter $σ_w^2$, and the fitness functional combines spectral agreement, marginal stability, and a symmetry-constrained critical anchor. Comparing three evolutionary models, we find that only the fully symmetry-constrained Ginibre $U(1)$ version robustly approaches a narrow near-marginal regime and reproduces the predicted low-frequency finite-width spectral behavior. These results support the use of symmetry-guided effective stability diagnostics as practical principles for stochastic architecture search in controlled settings.

### [356] [An explicit operator explains end-to-end computation in the modern neural networks used for sequence and language modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20595)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立SSM与非线性振荡器网络的数学对应关系；以S4D（对角线性时不变实现）为具体案例，将其嵌入环状网络拓扑；推导前向传播的封闭算子表达式，解析完整输入-输出映射。

Abstract: We establish a mathematical correspondence between state space models, a state-of-the-art architecture for capturing long-range dependencies in data, and an exactly solvable nonlinear oscillator network. As a specific example of this general correspondence, we analyze the diagonal linear time-invariant implementation of the Structured State Space Sequence model (S4). The correspondence embeds S4D, a specific implementation of S4, into a ring network topology, in which recent inputs are encoded, as waves of activity traveling over the one-dimensional spatial layout of the network. We then derive an exact operator expression for the full forward pass of S4D, yielding an analytical characterization of its complete input-output map. This expression reveals that the nonlinear decoder in the system induces interactions between these information-carrying waves that enable classifying real-world sequences. These results generalize across modern SSM architectures, and show that they admit an exact mathematical description with a clear physical interpretation. These insights enable a new level of interpretability for these systems in terms of nonlinear oscillator networks.

### [357] [Learning Hippo: Multi-attractor Dynamics and Stability Effects in a Biologically Detailed CA3 Extension of Hopfield Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20679)
*Daniele Corradetti,Renato Corradetti*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个生物细节丰富的CA3自联想记忆模型扩展，包含多种神经元类型、多区室、多规则可塑性及双模态胆碱能编码/巩固周期。在多种任务上评估后，该完整架构展现出三个经典霍普菲尔德模型不具备的定性特征：多吸引子交叉种行为、目标选择性联想回忆和降低的交叉种方差，且这些特征是架构特异的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典霍普菲尔德/马尔自联想记忆模型过于简化，缺乏生物真实性。作者旨在构建一个生物细节更丰富的CA3模型，探究生物细节是否带来经典模型不具备的 emergent 计算能力。

Method: 扩展经典CA3自联想记忆模型，引入十种神经元群体（两种不对称锥体亚型、八种GABA能中间神经元类别）、四十七个区室、多种可塑性规则（循环Hebb、BCM抗饱和、苔藓纤维短时程、内源性大麻素iLTD、爆发门控Hebb）以及双模态胆碱能编码/巩固周期。在N=256规模下，评估自联想、联想和时间序列模式完成能力，并控制抑制性比例进行对比。

Result: 完整架构在与最小霍普菲尔德基线对比中，展现出三个定性特征：(i) K=5时多吸引子交叉种行为，两个种子收敛到正吸引子（Cohen's d=0.71, p=0.08）；(ii) K≥5时目标选择性联想回忆，从A部分线索检索B而非回显A（Pearson margin Δ=+0.163）；(iii) 完整模型在干净上游下的交叉种方差低于最小基线（比值1.0-3.0）。这些特征在多个独立任务中一致出现，且最小基线中不存在。

Conclusion: 生物细节丰富的CA3模型展现出经典霍普菲尔德模型不具备的 emergent 计算能力，表明生物真实性对于理解海马记忆机制至关重要。这些架构特异的定性特征暗示生物细节可能赋予神经网络超越经典模型的计算优势。

Abstract: We present a biologically detailed extension of the classical Hopfield/Marr auto-associative memory model for CA3, implementing ten populations (two asymmetric pyramidal subtypes, eight GABAergic interneuron classes), forty-seven compartments, multi-rule plasticity (recurrent Hebb, BCM anti-saturation, mossy-fiber short-term, endocannabinoid iLTD, burst-gated Hebb), and a bimodal cholinergic encoding/consolidation cycle. Evaluated on pattern completion across auto-associative, associative, and temporal regimes, and on a controlled inhibitory-proportion manipulation at $N{=}256$, the full architecture exhibits \emph{three qualitative signatures absent from a minimal Hopfield baseline}: (i)~multi-attractor cross-seed behaviour at $K{=}5$ with biologically realistic inhibitory proportions, where two of five seeds converge to positive attractors with margin ${+}0.10{-}0.22$ (Cohen's $d{=}0.71$, one-sided $p{=}0.08$); (ii)~target-selective associative recall in paired $(A, B)$ memory at $K{\geq}5$, where the full model retrieves $B$ from a partial cue of $A$ while the minimal model echoes $A$ (Pearson margin $Δ{=}{+}0.163$ at $K{=}5$); (iii)~reduced cross-seed variance of the full model below the minimal baseline under clean upstream, with ratios $1.0{-}3.0$. These three signatures are architecture-specific: they appear consistently across independent regimes and are absent from the minimal control.

</details>
